## üîç Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### üéØ Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 100 page(s) - 100 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**Issue**: Target has insufficient size

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<a href="https://www.canada.ca/en.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">...</a>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/a
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/a')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://accessible.canada.ca/creating-accessibility-standards/can-asc-521-design-and-delivery-accessible-programs-and-services/10-support-person
- https://accessible.canada.ca/creating-accessibility-standards/canasc-en-301-5492024-accessibility-requirements-ict-products-and-services/12-documentation-and-support-services

#### Pattern 15: Affects 100 page(s) - 100 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

#### Rule: [SIA-R68: Accessible name contains the visible label text](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r68)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element owns no elements as required by its semantic role
- HTML: `<ul class="list-inline"> 																																																	...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@class="list-inline"]`

### https://accessible.canada.ca/creating-accessibility-standards/can-asc-282025-accessible-ready-housing/5-preface

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://accessibilite.canada.ca/elaboration-normes-accessibilite/can-asc-282025-logements-prets-laccessibilite/5-preface" class="language-link" lang="fr" hreflang="fr" data-drupal-link-system-path="node/726">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="language-link"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://www.canada.ca/en.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/sites/default/files/2025-06/standard-accessiblereadyhousing-2-8-2025.docx" class="file-download file-download-application file-download-vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document btn btn-primary" target="_blank" download="" title="Download word version">Word</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="file-download file-download-application file-download-vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document btn btn-primary"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a target="_blank" class="btn btn-dark cross-link" href="https://accessible.canada.ca/creating-accessibility-standards/summary-of-can-asc-282025-accessible-ready-housing">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="btn btn-dark cross-link"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is not allowed for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R56: Landmarks with the same role are distinguishable](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r56)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Some `navigation` have the same name.

#### Rule: [SIA-R61](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r61)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The document does not start with a level 1 heading

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="book-parent-label h1">CAN-ASC-2.8:2025 ‚Äì Accessible-Ready Housing</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="book-parent-label h1"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R74](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="book-parent-label h1">CAN-ASC-2.8:2025 ‚Äì Accessible-Ready Housing</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="book-parent-label h1"]`

## Detailed Failure Information (axe)

### https://accessible.canada.ca/creating-accessibility-standards/can-asc-521-design-and-delivery-accessible-programs-and-services/10-support-person

#### Rule: [aria-allowed-attr](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-attr?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must only use supported ARIA attributes
- HTML: `<div class="tgl-panel" aria-labelledby="wb-auto-3" aria-expanded="true" aria-hidden="false">`
- XPath: `div[aria-labelledby="wb-auto-3"]`

#### Rule: [aria-allowed-role](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-role?application=playwright)
**Impact**: minor

**Failure 1:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<details id="information" data-webform-details-nosave="true" data-once="details webform-details-save" open="open" class="wb-auto-2-grp fade in" role="tabpanel" aria-expanded="true" aria-labelledby="information-lnk">`
- XPath: `#information`

#### Rule: [aria-required-children](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-required-children?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Certain ARIA roles must contain particular children
- HTML: `<ul role="tablist" aria-live="off" class="generated" aria-hidden="false">`
- XPath: `.generated`

#### Rule: [landmark-unique](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-unique?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Landmarks should have a unique role or role/label/title (i.e. accessible name) combination
- HTML: `<nav>`
- XPath: `#nav-top > nav`

### https://accessible.canada.ca/creating-accessibility-standards/canasc-en-301-5492024-accessibility-requirements-ict-products-and-services/12-documentation-and-support-services

**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<input placeholder="Search this site" data-drupal-selector="edit-search-api-fulltext" class="form-text form-control" type="text" id="edit-search-api-fulltext" name="search_api_fulltext" value="" size="30" maxlength="128">`
- XPath: `#edit-search-api-fulltext`

#### Rule: [aria-required-children](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-required-children?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Certain ARIA roles must contain particular children
- HTML: `<ul role="tablist" aria-live="off" class="generated" aria-hidden="false">`

- Message: Landmarks should have a unique role or role/label/title (i.e. accessible name) combination

- XPath: `#nav-top > nav`

- XPath: `#information`

#### Rule: [color-contrast](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/color-contrast?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must only use supported ARIA attributes
- HTML: `<div class="tgl-panel" aria-labelledby="wb-auto-3" aria-expanded="true" aria-hidden="false">`
- XPath: `div[aria-labelledby="wb-auto-3"]`

#### Rule: [aria-allowed-role](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-role?application=playwright)

**Failure 1:**

- HTML: `<details id="information" data-webform-details-nosave="true" data-once="details webform-details-save" open="open" class="wb-auto-2-grp fade in" role="tabpanel" aria-expanded="true" aria-labelledby="information-lnk">`
- XPath: `#information`

#### Rule: [aria-required-children](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-required-children?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Certain ARIA roles must contain particular children
- HTML: `<ul role="tablist" aria-live="off" class="generated" aria-hidden="false">`
- XPath: `.generated`

### https://accessible.canada.ca/creating-accessibility-standards/can-asc-282025-accessible-ready-housing/8-references

#### Rule: [aria-allowed-attr](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-attr?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must only use supported ARIA attributes
- HTML: `<div class="tgl-panel" aria-labelledby="wb-auto-3" aria-expanded="true" aria-hidden="false">`
- XPath: `div[aria-labelledby="wb-auto-3"]`

#### Rule: [aria-allowed-role](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-role?application=playwright)
**Impact**: minor

**Failure 1:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<details id="information" data-webform-details-nosave="true" data-once="details webform-details-save" open="open" class="wb-auto-2-grp fade in" role="tabpanel" aria-expanded="true" aria-labelledby="information-lnk">`
- XPath: `#information`

#### Rule: [aria-required-children](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-required-children?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Certain ARIA roles must contain particular children
- HTML: `<ul role="tablist" aria-live="off" class="generated" aria-hidden="false">`
- XPath: `.generated`

#### Rule: [color-contrast](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/color-contrast?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<input placeholder="Search this site" data-drupal-selector="edit-search-api-fulltext" class="form-text form-control" type="text" id="edit-search-api-fulltext" name="search_api_fulltext" value="" size="30" maxlength="128">`
- XPath: `#edit-search-api-fulltext`

#### Rule: [landmark-unique](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-unique?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Landmarks should have a unique role or role/label/title (i.e. accessible name) combination
- HTML: `<nav>`
- XPath: `#nav-top > nav`
